======================================================================
LOADING HOT-PATH CANDIDATE AUDIT
======================================================================
Goal:
  Build a concrete candidate list for real loading speedups.
  Priority is synchronous file/map/list work, because worker-count changes broke completion queue contracts.


======================================================================
STARTUP / ASSET IO CANDIDATES
======================================================================

Candidate: ModelLoader::LoadFile
Reason: central startup asset scheduling path from earlier audit
